commit 6468f2faba3db5b3b858bd9472736f80669087c9
Author: Madhu Challa <challa@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Dec 1 12:49:35 2023 -0800

    Add support for 1.1 compat with openssl 3.x
    
    This package installs /etc/pki/openssl11.cnf that can be
    selected at process startup time via OPENSSL_CONF env
    
    For k8s it can be done via
              image: challa/opflex:11
              env:
              - name: OPENSSL_CONF
                value: "/etc/pki/openssl11.cnf"
    
    The variable makes the openssl3 libs compatible with 1.1
    If not set the behavior is same as openssl3
